                            <h4 class="mchp-tab-content-title">Your Privacy</h4>
                            <p>
                                Our cookies are free. In order to provide with the best
                                experience possible, we might sometimes track
                                information about you on our web site; we don’t sell
                                your information, but we use it to personalize your
                                web experience, track analytics and for target
                                advertising (which is really just telling you about our
                                latest products that meet your preferences).

                                some cookies you can choose not to allow. Click on
                                the different categories to find out more. Please note
                                that blocking some types of cookies may impact your
                                experience of the site and services we are able to offer.
                                Just like taking the chocolate chips out of your cookie.
                                It just doesn’t taste as good.
